antimonous acid  <-->  antimonite + 3 H+			antimonous acid // antimonite // H<SUP>+</SUP>
preuroporphyrinogen  ->  uroporphyrinogen-I + H2O			preuroporphyrinogen // uroporphyrinogen-I // H<sub>2</sub>O

keto-D-fructose 6-phosphate  <-->  beta-D-fructofuranose 6-phosphate			<i>keto</i>-D-fructose 6-phosphate // &beta;-D-fructofuranose 6-phosphate
